They have lots of One Of A Kind items, most of which are handmade by local residents. There are a lot of Long Beach themed items as well, so this is the perfect spot for unique souvenirs.

The staff here are friendly and helpful.

<Name>Christopher Jacob<//Name><Time>1431024567197<//Time><Rating>4</Rating><Text>Very nice little shop in downtown LB. The retail space is packed with local-made products ranging from handbags to pickled peppers! It's a fantastic place to pick up a gift for that special someone, or if you want to grab some premium goodies to support your local makers! I have my eye on their locally roasted coffee and hot sauce selection, but they also have soaps, candles, stationary and much more.

My only negative would be some of the prices were a bit ridiculous. I understand you get what you pay for, and honestly its worth it to know the money is going to some creative folks living in the city, however some tags were just gasp worthy! (Example: a small bag made of recycled material about a foot long by 8" high was priced at approx $250!! It was a nice bag, but not THAT nice!!)

I hope this shop stays open for a long time, its things like this that encourage folks to make their own goodies and sell to their community. Its an awesome idea with a beautiful execution.</Text>< Pics>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
MADE is a super cool shop servicing downtown Long Beach by carrying local makers of all sorts: jewelry, clothing, housewares, ceramics, doggie stuff, accessories, furniture, and lots of edibles like chocolate, sauces, teas/coffees, and more!

Downtown LB is small but mighty. The East Village has a small amount of local shoppery, but that's about it. MADE almost suffered the fate of many businesses that attempt to make it on Pine but with some creative and loving business dealings seems like it is putting down roots and will become a staple of DTLB.

The large space also hosts many community events like art shows, holiday parties, readings, polling, monthly/weekly pop-ups, and a lot of other creative and cool reasons to drop in.< /review>

I also loved my salted caramel with nuts ice cream. Very rich & appropriate after a long bike ride. The only downside was my spinach ravioli. There was barely any seasoning or flavouring. We went here on a Saturday afternoon and it wasn‚Äôt even packed. Made it the perfect pit stop. We ended up covering it in pepper to make it taste better. Other than the ravioli, everything was great!< /review>

< Review>
Great place with caring people, whether it's keeping your pets healthy or helping you say goodbye to a sick pet (we've done both). Always honest and up front about any costs for care before services are performed. You can request an appointment or ask a question online and someone will call you back promptly.  They're open 7 days a week, so I never have trouble finding an appointment that fits my schedule.  If you adopt from SD Humane, they honor the vet visit coupon that comes with your adoption.  I highly recommend this veterinary office.< /Review>

<Review>These guys care tremendously and I really loved having them as my vet. Came in with my little guy and he had pustules all in his ears and mouth, he also had a pretty high fever. They didn't recognize what it was initially but they put him on an antibiotic regime that helped pretty quickly, then they did a biopsy and a culture and it came back as Staph. <user>100255605768999117373<//user>< Name>
Ethan Wittenberg< /Name>
<Time>1613400261252< /Time><rate>5</rate>< Review>
We are brand new to fishing and came to this shop Saturday (2/13/2021) for some hooks and bait.
We thought we knew what we needed from talking to other people, but where obviously a little daunted by entering a shop with so many different options.
After bopping around the store for a little while, we were approached by a man named Ed. I am fairly sure that was his name, sorry if it's not!
Ed came out of nowhere like a shining beacon of light. Surely our requests where simple to people with such vast knowledge, but Ed showed extreme interest in helping us with our amateur fishing adventures.
He didn't play the old salesman trick of trying to sell us a bunch of things, he was just excited. Beyond showing us the best hooks/baits/ weights etc. He asked us were we planned to go and when, and offered an incredible amount of insight and help along the way.
Not once did I get the feeling that we were being judged for not knowing anything, nor did I feel intimated by him or anyone else at the shop. Just honest help and real enthusiasm.
So thanks a ton Ed and everyone at Bay Tackle. We will absolutely be back when we need supplies.
We didn't end up catching any fish that day but maybe that just means another excuse to come to this great shop.

* Also as a side note they took COVID very seriously and we felt safe shopping there forsure!<//Review>

< review>
New spot with an unusual concept. It's fun and interactive. You get to see your ice cream being made, and that is a treat. This place seems like a family run franchise, and they aren't without a few issues. But the focus is on the ice cream rolls. And while it's exciting and fun, the end product leaves you wanting. The texture is not all that it's made up to be. I would still stick to conventional ice cream.

Not a bad place, and one should experience this ice cream roll. At least once.< /review>

< review>

But after trying three different creations, I can say definitively that it is great ice cream! I tried the strawberry, the strawberry banana and the Oreo. This place stands out from other ice cream joints. If you are looking for something new to try, look no further! This can be a little pricey, but take the plunge, place your order, and enjoy the show! They will make your ice cream before your eyes -- these cups are truly works of art! <user>106559997972596259652</user><Name>Alex Dang< /Name>< Time>
1570121882689<//Time>
<rating>5< /rating>< text>
Are you kidding me?!? I'm reading so many reviews about price and portion sizes, lol. The small cup of ice cream was so worth the $7 bucks! The place gives a good-sized portion amount. And to be honest, you really shouldn't be eating anymore, lol.

Just because an ice cream place is in Oakland Chinatown doesn't mean it has to be cheap. For the effort and craftsman of the Instagram-able ice cream rolls, I'd definitely say it's worth the price tag.

My party and I went around 6 pm on a weeknight and got our orders within 15-20 minutes. I was just in "awe" with the artistry of making the delicious rolls.

I ordered the Purple Yam and my brother got the Matcha Green. I'd recommend both as they're both to die for. Super thick. Super creamy. Mhm. They were both just explosions of flavors.

Overall, I'd totally come here as this place was super delicious.

A few negatives to note:
- Cash only
- No line/name system</text>
